 	var ua = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
 	var s;
 	(s = ua.match(/rv:([\d.]+)\) like gecko/)) ? Sys.ie = s[1] :
 	(s = ua.match(/msie ([\d.]+)/)) ? Sys.ie = s[1] :
 	(s = ua.match(/firefox\/([\d.]+)/)) ? Sys.firefox = s[1] :
 	(s = ua.match(/chrome\/([\d.]+)/)) ? Sys.chrome = s[1] :
 	(s = ua.match(/opera.([\d.]+)/)) ? Sys.opera = s[1] :
 	(s = ua.match(/version\/([\d.]+).*safari/)) ? Sys.safari = s[1] : 0;
 				
 	if (Sys.ie == '8.0' || Sys.ie == '7.0' || Sys.ie == '6.0' ){ 
 		alert('We are sorry that the current version of your browser is not compatible with our website. Please update it to Internet Explorer 9 or later. Alternatively use Google Chrome or Firefox for the completed view. Thank you!');

     var Sys = {};
 	var ua = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
 	var s;
 	(s = ua.match(/rv:([\d.]+)\) like gecko/)) ? Sys.ie = s[1] :
 	(s = ua.match(/msie ([\d.]+)/)) ? Sys.ie = s[1] :
 	(s = ua.match(/firefox\/([\d.]+)/)) ? Sys.firefox = s[1] :
 	(s = ua.match(/chrome\/([\d.]+)/)) ? Sys.chrome = s[1] :
 	(s = ua.match(/opera.([\d.]+)/)) ? Sys.opera = s[1] :
 	(s = ua.match(/version\/([\d.]+).*safari/)) ? Sys.safari = s[1] : 0;
 				
 	if (Sys.ie == '8.0' || Sys.ie == '7.0' || Sys.ie == '6.0' ){ 
 		alert('We are sorry that the current version of your browser is not compatible with our website. Please update it to Internet Explorer 9 or later. Alternatively use Google Chrome or Firefox for the completed view. Thank you!');

 	var s;
 	(s = ua.match(/rv:([\d.]+)\) like gecko/)) ? Sys.ie = s[1] :
 	(s = ua.match(/msie ([\d.]+)/)) ? Sys.ie = s[1] :
 	(s = ua.match(/firefox\/([\d.]+)/)) ? Sys.firefox = s[1] :
 	(s = ua.match(/chrome\/([\d.]+)/)) ? Sys.chrome = s[1] :
 	(s = ua.match(/opera.([\d.]+)/)) ? Sys.opera = s[1] :
 	(s = ua.match(/version\/([\d.]+).*safari/)) ? Sys.safari = s[1] : 0;
 				
 	if (Sys.ie == '8.0' || Sys.ie == '7.0' || Sys.ie == '6.0' ){
